I've uploaded a python code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
The latest value, instead of the previous value,  is provided in $effect teardown if the state is a $derived
### Describe the bug

Not sure if this is a bug or intended. According to [this breaking change](https://github.com/sveltejs/svelte/pull/15469), if the state caused an $effect to rerun, Svelte should provide the previous value of the state in the teardown function. This work for $state currently, but not for $derived, though it does work if $derived is reassigned. 

### Reproduction

https://svelte.dev/playground/untitled?version=5.33.18#H4sIAAAAAAAACnWPy2rEMAxFf8WIgcl0woSuCm4SmC_oqqumizyU1tRVjKVkOgT_e3HS92MldHSPZM9A9TOChlsSIxY7SKE3Fhn03QxydnEWAaTvyaNzB57QSmRNzfgXbwcSJGHQkHPrjZOyokosimJVqA1LLZhc7q4_6II79GbCLuELXkZUyQb7HltJkp0qSjVHVEk7EA8WD3Z4SLaPRjFrtU0Vr5ZU4lFGT-qb9ENrzvjbC7GEXUV59vlsyptRZCA1UGtN-1TM617e70N57DrFebYmyv-z8X9XobyZ0J-8kXj7q-VK1mrmkGfurV36FUAKgi8CWvyI4T4FqY09GepA97VlDK_x94v_xwEAAA==


### System Info

```shell
Svelte playground (5.33.18)
Chrome 137.0.7151.56
```

### Severity

annoyance
Incorrect prop value in onDestroy when there's a setter but not getter in the template
### Describe the bug

When a prop has a setter (for instance `<button onclick={() => (checked = !checked)}></button>`) but it doesn't have a getter (like `<p>{checked}</p>`), the value read during `onDestroy` does not match either the old or the current value of the prop, it's instead read as `null`.

This happens because the compiler decides to use `$.prop` to read the prop since it detects a "setter", `$.prop` "wraps" the prop in a `derived` but since we never read from it, when we execute `onDestroy` the `derived` is still in an "uninitialized" state hence it returns `null` instead of the correct value. 

### Reproduction

https://svelte.dev/playground/4fa745c18a3c41e88bda761f37b36783?version=5.34.9

Click `count++` twice, the 2nd time the `Component` is unmounted and `onDestroy` is called and it will log the incorrect `checked` value that should be `true` but is logged as `null`.

    46	/**
    47	 * @param {'$effect' | '$effect.pre' | '$inspect'} rune
    48	 */
    49	export function validate_effect(rune) {
    50	        if (active_effect === null && active_reaction === null) {
    51	                e.effect_orphan(rune);
    52	        }
    53	
    54	        if (active_reaction !== null && (active_reaction.f & UNOWNED) !== 0 && active_effect === null) {
    55	                e.effect_in_unowned_derived();
    56	        }
    57	
    58	        if (is_destroying_effect) {
    59	                e.effect_in_teardown(rune);
    60	        }
    61	}
    62	
    63	/**
    64	 * @param {Effect} effect
    65	 * @param {Effect} parent_effect
    66	 */
    67	function push_effect(effect, parent_effect) {
    68	        var parent_last = parent_effect.last;
    69	        if (parent_last === null) {
    70	                parent_effect.last = parent_effect.first = effect;
    71	        } else {
    72	                parent_last.next = effect;
    73	                effect.prev = parent_last;
    74	                parent_effect.last = effect;
    75	        }
    76	}
    77	
    78	/**
    79	 * @param {number} type
    80	 * @param {null | (() => void | (() => void))} fn
    81	 * @param {boolean} sync
    82	 * @param {boolean} push
    83	 * @returns {Effect}
    84	 */
    85	function create_effect(type, fn, sync, push = true) {
    86	        var parent = active_effect;
    87	
    88	        if (DEV) {
    89	                // Ensure the parent is never an inspect effect
    90	                while (parent !== null && (parent.f & INSPECT_EFFECT) !== 0) {
    91	                        parent = parent.parent;
    92	                }
    93	        }
    94	
    95	        /** @type {Effect} */
    96	        var effect = {
    97	                ctx: component_context,
    98	                deps: null,
    99	                nodes_start: null,
   100	                nodes_end: null,
   101	                f: type | DIRTY,
   102	                first: null,
   103	                fn,
   104	                last: null,
   105	                next: null,
   106	                parent,
   107	                prev: null,
   108	                teardown: null,
   109	                transitions: null,
   110	                wv: 0,
   111	                ac: null
   112	        };
   113	
   114	        if (DEV) {
   115	                effect.component_function = dev_current_component_function;
   116	        }
   117	
   118	        if (sync) {
   119	                try {
   120	                        update_effect(effect);
   121	                        effect.f |= EFFECT_RAN;
   122	                } catch (e) {
   123	                        destroy_effect(effect);
   124	                        throw e;
   125	                }
   126	        } else if (fn !== null) {
   127	                schedule_effect(effect);
   128	        }
   129	
   130	        // if an effect has no dependencies, no DOM and no teardown function,
   131	        // don't bother adding it to the effect tree
   132	        var inert =
   133	                sync &&
   134	                effect.deps === null &&
   135	                effect.first === null &&
   136	                effect.nodes_start === null &&
   137	                effect.teardown === null &&
   138	                (effect.f & (EFFECT_HAS_DERIVED | BOUNDARY_EFFECT)) === 0;
   139	
   140	        if (!inert && push) {
   141	                if (parent !== null) {
   142	                        push_effect(effect, parent);
   143	                }
   144	
   145	                // if we're in a derived, add the effect there too
   146	                if (active_reaction !== null && (active_reaction.f & DERIVED) !== 0) {
   147	                        var derived = /** @type {Derived} */ (active_reaction);
   148	                        (derived.effects ??= []).push(effect);
   149	                }
   150	        }
   151	
   152	        return effect;
   153	}
   154	
   155	/**
   156	 * Internal representation of `$effect.tracking()`
   157	 * @returns {boolean}
   158	 */
   159	export function effect_tracking() {
   160	        return active_reaction !== null && !untracking;
   161	}
   162	
   163	/**
   164	 * @param {() => void} fn
   165	 */
   166	export function teardown(fn) {
   167	        const effect = create_effect(RENDER_EFFECT, null, false);
   168	        set_signal_status(effect, CLEAN);
   169	        effect.teardown = fn;
   170	        return effect;
   171	}
   172	
   173	/**
   174	 * Internal representation of `$effect(...)`
   175	 * @param {() => void | (() => void)} fn
   176	 */
   177	export function user_effect(fn) {
   178	        validate_effect('$effect');
   179	
   180	        // Non-nested `$effect(...)` in a component should be deferred
   181	        // until the component is mounted
   182	        var defer =
   183	                active_effect !== null &&
   184	                (active_effect.f & BRANCH_EFFECT) !== 0 &&
   185	                component_context !== null &&
   186	                !component_context.m;
   187	
   188	        if (DEV) {
   189	                define_property(fn, 'name', {
   190	                        value: '$effect'
   191	                });
   192	        }
   193	
   194	        if (defer) {
   195	                var context = /** @type {ComponentContext} */ (component_context);
   196	                (context.e ??= []).push({
   197	                        fn,
   198	                        effect: active_effect,
   199	                        reaction: active_reaction
   200	                });
   201	        } else {
   202	                var signal = effect(fn);
   203	                return signal;
   204	        }
   205	}
   206	
   207	/**
   208	 * Internal representation of `$effect.pre(...)`
   209	 * @param {() => void | (() => void)} fn
   210	 * @returns {Effect}
   211	 */
   212	export function user_pre_effect(fn) {
   213	        validate_effect('$effect.pre');
   214	        if (DEV) {
   215	                define_property(fn, 'name', {
   216	                        value: '$effect.pre'
   217	                });
   218	        }
   219	        return render_effect(fn);
   220	}
   221	
   222	/** @param {() => void | (() => void)} fn */
   223	export function inspect_effect(fn) {
   224	        return create_effect(INSPECT_EFFECT, fn, true);
   225	}
   226	
   227	/**
   228	 * Internal representation of `$effect.root(...)`
   229	 * @param {() => void | (() => void)} fn
   230	 * @returns {() => void}
   231	 */
   232	export function effect_root(fn) {
   233	        const effect = create_effect(ROOT_EFFECT, fn, true);
   234	
   235	        return () => {
   236	                destroy_effect(effect);
   237	        };
   238	}
   239	
   240	/**
   241	 * An effect root whose children can transition out
   242	 * @param {() => void} fn
   243	 * @returns {(options?: { outro?: boolean }) => Promise<void>}
   244	 */
   245	export function component_root(fn) {
   246	        const effect = create_effect(ROOT_EFFECT, fn, true);
   247	
   248	        return (options = {}) => {
   249	                return new Promise((fulfil) => {
   250	                        if (options.outro) {
   251	                                pause_effect(effect, () => {
   252	                                        destroy_effect(effect);
   253	                                        fulfil(undefined);
   254	                                });
   255	                        } else {
   256	                                destroy_effect(effect);
   257	                                fulfil(undefined);
   258	                        }
   259	                });
   260	        };
   261	}
   262	
   263	/**
   264	 * @param {() => void | (() => void)} fn
   265	 * @returns {Effect}
   266	 */
   267	export function effect(fn) {
   268	        return create_effect(EFFECT, fn, false);
   269	}
   270	
   271	/**
   272	 * Internal representation of `$: ..`
   273	 * @param {() => any} deps
   274	 * @param {() => void | (() => void)} fn
   275	 */
   276	export function legacy_pre_effect(deps, fn) {
   277	        var context = /** @type {ComponentContextLegacy} */ (component_context);
   278	
   279	        /** @type {{ effect: null | Effect, ran: boolean }} */
   280	        var token = { effect: null, ran: false };
   281	        context.l.r1.push(token);
   282	
   283	        token.effect = render_effect(() => {
   284	                deps();
   285	
   286	                // If this legacy pre effect has already run before the end of the reset, then
   287	                // bail out to emulate the same behavior.
   288	                if (token.ran) return;
   289	
   290	                token.ran = true;
   291	                set(context.l.r2, true);
   292	                untrack(fn);
   293	        });
   294	}
   295	
   296	export function legacy_pre_effect_reset() {
   297	        var context = /** @type {ComponentContextLegacy} */ (component_context);
   298	
   299	        render_effect(() => {
   300	                if (!get(context.l.r2)) return;
   301	
   302	                // Run dirty `$:` statements
   303	                for (var token of context.l.r1) {
   304	                        var effect = token.effect;
   305	
   306	                        // If the effect is CLEAN, then make it MAYBE_DIRTY. This ensures we traverse through
   307	                        // the effects dependencies and correctly ensure each dependency is up-to-date.
   308	                        if ((effect.f & CLEAN) !== 0) {
   309	                                set_signal_status(effect, MAYBE_DIRTY);
   310	                        }
   311	
   312	                        if (check_dirtiness(effect)) {
   313	                                update_effect(effect);
   314	                        }
   315	
   316	                        token.ran = false;
   317	                }
   318	
   319	                context.l.r2.v = false; // set directly to avoid rerunning this effect
   320	        });
   321	}
   322	
   323	/**
   324	 * @param {() => void | (() => void)} fn
   325	 * @returns {Effect}
   326	 */
   327	export function render_effect(fn) {
   328	        return create_effect(RENDER_EFFECT, fn, true);
   329	}
   330	
   331	/**
   332	 * @param {(...expressions: any) => void | (() => void)} fn
   333	 * @param {Array<() => any>} thunks
   334	 * @param {<T>(fn: () => T) => Derived<T>} d
   335	 * @returns {Effect}
   336	 */
   337	export function template_effect(fn, thunks = [], d = derived) {
   338	        if (DEV) {
   339	                // wrap the effect so that we can decorate stack trace with `in {expression}`
   340	                // (TODO maybe there's a better approach?)
   341	                return render_effect(() => {
   342	                        var outer = /** @type {Effect} */ (active_effect);
   343	                        var inner = () => fn(...deriveds.map(get));
   344	
   345	                        define_property(outer.fn, 'name', { value: '{expression}' });
   346	                        define_property(inner, 'name', { value: '{expression}' });
   347	
   348	                        const deriveds = thunks.map(d);
   349	                        block(inner);
   350	                });
   351	        }
   352	
   353	        const deriveds = thunks.map(d);
   354	        return block(() => fn(...deriveds.map(get)));
   355	}
   356	
   357	/**
   358	 * @param {(() => void)} fn
   359	 * @param {number} flags
   360	 */
   361	export function block(fn, flags = 0) {
   362	        var effect = create_effect(RENDER_EFFECT | BLOCK_EFFECT | flags, fn, true);
   363	        if (DEV) {
   364	                effect.dev_stack = dev_stack;
   365	        }
   366	        return effect;
   367	}
   368	
   369	/**
   370	 * @param {(() => void)} fn
   371	 * @param {boolean} [push]
   372	 */
   373	export function branch(fn, push = true) {
   374	        return create_effect(RENDER_EFFECT | BRANCH_EFFECT, fn, true, push);
   375	}
   376	
   377	/**
   378	 * @param {Effect} effect
   379	 */
   380	export function execute_effect_teardown(effect) {
   381	        var teardown = effect.teardown;
   382	        if (teardown !== null) {
   383	                const previously_destroying_effect = is_destroying_effect;
   384	                const previous_reaction = active_reaction;
   385	                set_is_destroying_effect(true);
   386	                set_active_reaction(null);
   387	                try {
   388	                        teardown.call(null);
   389	                } finally {
   390	                        set_is_destroying_effect(previously_destroying_effect);
   391	                        set_active_reaction(previous_reaction);
   392	                }
   393	        }
   394	}
   395	
   396	/**
   397	 * @param {Effect} signal
   398	 * @param {boolean} remove_dom
   399	 * @returns {void}
   400	 */
   401	export function destroy_effect_children(signal, remove_dom = false) {
   402	        var effect = signal.first;
   403	        signal.first = signal.last = null;
   404	
   405	        while (effect !== null) {
   406	                effect.ac?.abort(STALE_REACTION);
   407	
   408	                var next = effect.next;
   409	
   410	                if ((effect.f & ROOT_EFFECT) !== 0) {
   411	                        // this is now an independent root
   412	                        effect.parent = null;
   413	                } else {
   414	                        destroy_effect(effect, remove_dom);
   415	                }
   416	
   417	                effect = next;
   418	        }
   419	}
   420	
   421	/**
   422	 * @param {Effect} signal
   423	 * @returns {void}
   424	 */
   425	export function destroy_block_effect_children(signal) {
   426	        var effect = signal.first;
   427	
   428	        while (effect !== null) {
   429	                var next = effect.next;
   430	                if ((effect.f & BRANCH_EFFECT) === 0) {
   431	                        destroy_effect(effect);
   432	                }
   433	                effect = next;
   434	        }
   435	}
   436	
   437	/**
   438	 * @param {Effect} effect
   439	 * @param {boolean} [remove_dom]
   440	 * @returns {void}
   441	 */
   442	export function destroy_effect(effect, remove_dom = true) {
   443	        var removed = false;
   444	
   445	        if (
   446	                (remove_dom || (effect.f & HEAD_EFFECT) !== 0) &&
   447	                effect.nodes_start !== null &&
   448	                effect.nodes_end !== null
   449	        ) {
   450	                remove_effect_dom(effect.nodes_start, /** @type {TemplateNode} */ (effect.nodes_end));
   451	                removed = true;
   452	        }
   453	
   454	        destroy_effect_children(effect, remove_dom && !removed);
   455	        remove_reactions(effect, 0);
   456	        set_signal_status(effect, DESTROYED);
   457	
   458	        var transitions = effect.transitions;
   459	
   460	        if (transitions !== null) {
   461	                for (const transition of transitions) {
   462	                        transition.stop();
   463	                }
   464	        }
   465	
   466	        execute_effect_teardown(effect);
   467	
   468	        var parent = effect.parent;
   469	
   470	        // If the parent doesn't have any children, then skip this work altogether
   471	        if (parent !== null && parent.first !== null) {
   472	                unlink_effect(effect);
   473	        }
   474	
   475	        if (DEV) {
   476	                effect.component_function = null;
   477	        }
   478	
   479	        // `first` and `child` are nulled out in destroy_effect_children
   480	        // we don't null out `parent` so that error propagation can work correctly
   481	        effect.next =
   482	                effect.prev =
   483	                effect.teardown =
   484	                effect.ctx =
   485	                effect.deps =
   486	                effect.fn =
   487	                effect.nodes_start =
   488	                effect.nodes_end =
   489	                effect.ac =
   490	                        null;
   491	}
   492	
   493	/**
   494	 *
   495	 * @param {TemplateNode | null} node
   496	 * @param {TemplateNode} end
   497	 */
   498	export function remove_effect_dom(node, end) {
   499	        while (node !== null) {
   500	                /** @type {TemplateNode | null} */
   501	                var next = node === end ? null : /** @type {TemplateNode} */ (get_next_sibling(node));
   502	
   503	                node.remove();
   504	                node = next;
   505	        }
   506	}
   507	
   508	/**
   509	 * Detach an effect from the effect tree, freeing up memory and
   510	 * reducing the amount of work that happens on subsequent traversals
   511	 * @param {Effect} effect
   512	 */
   513	export function unlink_effect(effect) {
   514	        var parent = effect.parent;
   515	        var prev = effect.prev;
   516	        var next = effect.next;
   517	
   518	        if (prev !== null) prev.next = next;
   519	        if (next !== null) next.prev = prev;
   520	
   521	        if (parent !== null) {
   522	                if (parent.first === effect) parent.first = next;
   523	                if (parent.last === effect) parent.last = prev;
   524	        }
   525	}
   526	
   527	/**
   528	 * When a block effect is removed, we don't immediately destroy it or yank it
   529	 * out of the DOM, because it might have transitions. Instead, we 'pause' it.
   530	 * It stays around (in memory, and in the DOM) until outro transitions have
   531	 * completed, and if the state change is reversed then we _resume_ it.
   532	 * A paused effect does not update, and the DOM subtree becomes inert.
   533	 * @param {Effect} effect
   534	 * @param {() => void} [callback]
   535	 */
   536	export function pause_effect(effect, callback) {
   537	        /** @type {TransitionManager[]} */
   538	        var transitions = [];
   539	
   540	        pause_children(effect, transitions, true);
   541	
   542	        run_out_transitions(transitions, () => {
   543	                destroy_effect(effect);
   544	                if (callback) callback();
   545	        });
   546	}
   547	
   548	/**
   549	 * @param {TransitionManager[]} transitions
   550	 * @param {() => void} fn
   551	 */
   552	export function run_out_transitions(transitions, fn) {
   553	        var remaining = transitions.length;
   554	        if (remaining > 0) {
   555	                var check = () => --remaining || fn();
   556	                for (var transition of transitions) {
   557	                        transition.out(check);
   558	                }
   559	        } else {
   560	                fn();
   561	        }
   562	}
   563	
   564	/**
   565	 * @param {Effect} effect
   566	 * @param {TransitionManager[]} transitions
   567	 * @param {boolean} local
   568	 */
   569	export function pause_children(effect, transitions, local) {
   570	        if ((effect.f & INERT) !== 0) return;
   571	        effect.f ^= INERT;
   572	
   573	        if (effect.transitions !== null) {
   574	                for (const transition of effect.transitions) {
   575	                        if (transition.is_global || local) {
   576	                                transitions.push(transition);
   577	                        }
   578	                }
   579	        }
   580	
   581	        var child = effect.first;
   582	
   583	        while (child !== null) {
   584	                var sibling = child.next;
   585	                var transparent = (child.f & EFFECT_TRANSPARENT) !== 0 || (child.f & BRANCH_EFFECT) !== 0;
   586	                // TODO we don't need to call pause_children recursively with a linked list in place
   587	                // it's slightly more involved though as we have to account for `transparent` changing
   588	                // through the tree.
   589	                pause_children(child, transitions, transparent ? local : false);
   590	                child = sibling;
   591	        }
   592	}
   593	
   594	/**
   595	 * The opposite of `pause_effect`. We call this if (for example)
   596	 * `x` becomes falsy then truthy: `{#if x}...{/if}`
   597	 * @param {Effect} effect
   598	 */
   599	export function resume_effect(effect) {
   600	        resume_children(effect, true);
   601	}
   602	
   603	/**
   604	 * @param {Effect} effect
   605	 * @param {boolean} local
   606	 */
   607	function resume_children(effect, local) {
   608	        if ((effect.f & INERT) === 0) return;
   609	        effect.f ^= INERT;
   610	
   611	        var child = effect.first;
   612	
   613	        while (child !== null) {
   614	                var sibling = child.next;
   615	                var transparent = (child.f & EFFECT_TRANSPARENT) !== 0 || (child.f & BRANCH_EFFECT) !== 0;
   616	                // TODO we don't need to call resume_children recursively with a linked list in place
   617	                // it's slightly more involved though as we have to account for `transparent` changing
   618	                // through the tree.
   619	                resume_children(child, transparent ? local : false);
   620	                child = sibling;
   621	        }
   622	
   623	        if (effect.transitions !== null) {
   624	                for (const transition of effect.transitions) {
   625	                        if (transition.is_global || local) {
   626	                                transition.in();
   627	                        }
   628	                }
   629	        }
   630	}
   631

   226	/**
   227	 * @param {Value} signal
   228	 * @param {Effect} effect

   230	 */
   231	function schedule_possible_effect_self_invalidation(signal, effect, root = true) {
   232	        var reactions = signal.reactions;
   233	        if (reactions === null) return;
   234	
   235	        for (var i = 0; i < reactions.length; i++) {

   237	
   238	                if (reaction_sources?.[1].includes(signal) && reaction_sources[0] === active_reaction) continue;
   239	
   240	                if ((reaction.f & DERIVED) !== 0) {
   241	                        schedule_possible_effect_self_invalidation(/** @type {Derived} */ (reaction), effect, false);
   242	                } else if (effect === reaction) {
   243	                        if (root) {
   244	                                set_signal_status(reaction, DIRTY);
   245	                        } else if ((reaction.f & CLEAN) !== 0) {
   246	                                set_signal_status(reaction, MAYBE_DIRTY);
   247	                        }
   248	                        schedule_effect(/** @type {Effect} */ (reaction));
   249	                }
   250	        }
   251	}
   252	
   253	/** @param {Reaction} reaction */
   254	export function update_reaction(reaction) {
   255	        var previous_deps = new_deps;
   256	        var previous_skipped_deps = skipped_deps;
   257	        var previous_untracked_writes = untracked_writes;
   258	        var previous_reaction = active_reaction;
   259	        var previous_skip_reaction = skip_reaction;
   260	        var previous_reaction_sources = reaction_sources;
   261	        var previous_component_context = component_context;
   262	        var previous_untracking = untracking;
   263	
   264	        var flags = reaction.f;
   265	
   266	        new_deps = /** @type {null | Value[]} */ (null);
   267	        skipped_deps = 0;
   268	        untracked_writes = null;
   269	        skip_reaction =
   270	                (flags & UNOWNED) !== 0 && (untracking || !is_updating_effect || active_reaction === null);
   271	        active_reaction = (flags & (BRANCH_EFFECT | ROOT_EFFECT)) === 0 ? reaction : null;
   272	
   273	        reaction_sources = null;
   274	        set_component_context(reaction.ctx);
   275	        untracking = false;
   276	        read_version++;
   277	
   278	        reaction.f |= EFFECT_IS_UPDATING;
   279	
   280	        if (reaction.ac !== null) {
   281	                reaction.ac.abort(STALE_REACTION);
   282	                reaction.ac = null;
   283	        }
   284	
   285	        try {
   286	                var result = /** @type {Function} */ (0, reaction.fn)();
   287	                var deps = reaction.deps;
   288	
   289	                if (new_deps !== null) {
   290	                        var i;
   291	
   292	                        remove_reactions(reaction, skipped_deps);
   293	
   294	                        if (deps !== null && skipped_deps > 0) {
   295	                                deps.length = skipped_deps + new_deps.length;
   296	                                for (i = 0; i < new_deps.length; i++) {
   297	                                        deps[skipped_deps + i] = new_deps[i];
   298	                                }
   299	                        } else {
   300	                                reaction.deps = deps = new_deps;
   301	                        }
   302	
   303	                        if (
   304	                                !skip_reaction ||
   305	                                // Deriveds that already have reactions can cleanup, so we still add them as reactions
   306	                                ((flags & DERIVED) !== 0 &&
   307	                                        /** @type {import('#client').Derived} */ (reaction).reactions !== null)
   308	                        ) {
   309	                                for (i = skipped_deps; i < deps.length; i++) {
   310	                                        (deps[i].reactions ??= []).push(reaction);
   311	                                }
   312	                        }
   313	                } else if (deps !== null && skipped_deps < deps.length) {
   314	                        remove_reactions(reaction, skipped_deps);
   315	                        deps.length = skipped_deps;
   316	                }
   317	
   318	                // If we're inside an effect and we have untracked writes, then we need to
   319	                // ensure that if any of those untracked writes result in re-invalidation
   320	                // of the current effect, then that happens accordingly
   321	                if (
   322	                        is_runes() &&
   323	                        untracked_writes !== null &&
   324	                        !untracking &&
   325	                        deps !== null &&
   326	                        (reaction.f & (DERIVED | MAYBE_DIRTY | DIRTY)) === 0
   327	                ) {
   328	                        for (i = 0; i < /** @type {Source[]} */ (untracked_writes).length; i++) {
   329	                                schedule_possible_effect_self_invalidation(
   330	                                        untracked_writes[i],
   331	                                        /** @type {Effect} */ (reaction)
   332	                                );
   333	                        }
   334	                }
   335	
   336	                // If we are returning to an previous reaction then
   337	                // we need to increment the read version to ensure that
   338	                // any dependencies in this reaction aren't marked with
   339	                // the same version
   340	                if (previous_reaction !== null && previous_reaction !== reaction) {
   341	                        read_version++;
   342	
   343	                        if (untracked_writes !== null) {
   344	                                if (previous_untracked_writes === null) {
   345	                                        previous_untracked_writes = untracked_writes;
   346	                                } else {
   347	                                        previous_untracked_writes.push(.../** @type {Source[]} */ (untracked_writes));
   348	                                }
   349	                        }
   350	                }
   351	
   352	                return result;
   353	        } catch (error) {
   354	                handle_error(error);
   355	        } finally {
   356	                new_deps = previous_deps;
   357	                skipped_deps = previous_skipped_deps;
   358	                untracked_writes = previous_untracked_writes;
   359	                active_reaction = previous_reaction;
   360	                skip_reaction = previous_skip_reaction;
   361	                reaction_sources = previous_reaction_sources;
   362	                set_component_context(previous_component_context);
   363	                untracking = previous_untracking;
   364	
   365	                reaction.f ^= EFFECT_IS_UPDATING;
   366	        }
   367	}
   368	
   369	/**
   370	 * @template V
   371	 * @param {Reaction} signal
   372	 * @param {Value<V>} dependency
   373	 * @returns {void}
   374	 */
   375	function remove_reaction(signal, dependency) {
   376	        let reactions = dependency.reactions;
   377	        if (reactions !== null) {
   378	                var index = index_of.call(reactions, signal);
   379	                if (index !== -1) {
   380	                        var new_length = reactions.length - 1;
   381	                        if (new_length === 0) {
   382	                                reactions = dependency.reactions = null;
   383	                        } else {
   384	                                // Swap with last element and then remove.
   385	                                reactions[index] = reactions[new_length];
   386	                                reactions.pop();
   387	                        }
   388	                }
   389	        }
   390	        // If the derived has no reactions, then we can disconnect it from the graph,
   391	        // allowing it to either reconnect in the future, or be GC'd by the VM.
   392	        if (
   393	                reactions === null &&
   394	                (dependency.f & DERIVED) !== 0 &&
   395	                // Destroying a child effect while updating a parent effect can cause a dependency to appear
   396	                // to be unused, when in fact it is used by the currently-updating parent. Checking `new_deps`
   397	                // allows us to skip the expensive work of disconnecting and immediately reconnecting it
   398	                (new_deps === null || !new_deps.includes(dependency))
   399	        ) {
   400	                set_signal_status(dependency, MAYBE_DIRTY);

    42	/**
    43	 * The proxy handler for rest props (i.e. `const { x, ...rest } = $props()`).
    44	 * Is passed the full `$$props` object and excludes the named props.
    45	 * @type {ProxyHandler<{ props: Record<string | symbol, unknown>, exclude: Array<string | symbol>, name?: string }>}}
    46	 */
    47	const rest_props_handler = {
    48	        get(target, key) {
    49	                if (target.exclude.includes(key)) return;
    50	                return target.props[key];
    51	        },
    52	        set(target, key) {
    53	                if (DEV) {
    54	                        // TODO should this happen in prod too?
    55	                        e.props_rest_readonly(`${target.name}.${String(key)}`);
    56	                }
    57	
    58	                return false;
    59	        },
    60	        getOwnPropertyDescriptor(target, key) {
    61	                if (target.exclude.includes(key)) return;
    62	                if (key in target.props) {
    63	                        return {
    64	                                enumerable: true,
    65	                                configurable: true,
    66	                                value: target.props[key]
    67	                        };
    68	                }
    69	        },
    70	        has(target, key) {
    71	                if (target.exclude.includes(key)) return false;
    72	                return key in target.props;
    73	        },
    74	        ownKeys(target) {
    75	                return Reflect.ownKeys(target.props).filter((key) => !target.exclude.includes(key));
    76	        }
    77	};

    85	/*#__NO_SIDE_EFFECTS__*/
    86	export function rest_props(props, exclude, name) {
    87	        return new Proxy(

    93	/**
    94	 * The proxy handler for legacy $$restProps and $$props

    96	 */
    97	const legacy_rest_props_handler = {
    98	        get(target, key) {
    99	                if (target.exclude.includes(key)) return;
   100	                get(target.version);
   101	                return key in target.special ? target.special[key]() : target.props[key];
   102	        },
   103	        set(target, key, value) {

   106	                        /** @type {Record<string, (v?: unknown) => unknown>} */

   120	                return true;
   121	        },

   157	/**
   158	 * The proxy handler for spread props. Handles the incoming array of props
   159	 * that looks like `() => { dynamic: props }, { static: prop }, ..` and wraps
   160	 * them so that the whole thing is passed to the component as the `$$props` argument.
   161	 * @template {Record<string | symbol, unknown>} T
   162	 * @type {ProxyHandler<{ props: Array<T | (() => T)> }>}}
   163	 */
   164	const spread_props_handler = {
   165	        get(target, key) {
   166	                let i = target.props.length;
   167	                while (i--) {
   168	                        let p = target.props[i];
   169	                        if (is_function(p)) p = p();
   170	                        if (typeof p === 'object' && p !== null && key in p) return p[key];
   171	                }
   172	        },
   173	        set(target, key, value) {
   174	                let i = target.props.length;
   175	                while (i--) {
   176	                        let p = target.props[i];
   177	                        if (is_function(p)) p = p();
   178	                        const desc = get_descriptor(p, key);
   179	                        if (desc && desc.set) {
   180	                                desc.set(value);
   181	                                return true;
   182	                        }
   183	                }
   184	                return false;
   185	        },
   186	        getOwnPropertyDescriptor(target, key) {
   187	                let i = target.props.length;
   188	                while (i--) {
   189	                        let p = target.props[i];
   190	                        if (is_function(p)) p = p();
   191	                        if (typeof p === 'object' && p !== null && key in p) {
   192	                                const descriptor = get_descriptor(p, key);
   193	                                if (descriptor && !descriptor.configurable) {
   194	                                        // Prevent a "Non-configurability Report Error": The target is an array, it does
   195	                                        // not actually contain this property. If it is now described as non-configurable,
   196	                                        // the proxy throws a validation error. Setting it to true avoids that.
   197	                                        descriptor.configurable = true;
   198	                                }
   199	                                return descriptor;
   200	                        }
   201	                }
   202	        },
   203	        has(target, key) {
   204	                // To prevent a false positive `is_entry_props` in the `prop` function
   205	                if (key === STATE_SYMBOL || key === LEGACY_PROPS) return false;
   206	
   207	                for (let p of target.props) {
   208	                        if (is_function(p)) p = p();
   209	                        if (p != null && key in p) return true;
   210	                }
   211	
   212	                return false;
   213	        },
   214	        ownKeys(target) {
   215	                /** @type {Array<string | symbol>} */
   216	                const keys = [];
   217	
   218	                for (let p of target.props) {
   219	                        if (is_function(p)) p = p();
   220	                        if (!p) continue;
   221	
   222	                        for (const key in p) {
   223	                                if (!keys.includes(key)) keys.push(key);
   224	                        }
   225	
   226	                        for (const key of Object.getOwnPropertySymbols(p)) {
   227	                                if (!keys.includes(key)) keys.push(key);
   228	                        }
   229	                }
   230	
   231	                return keys;
   232	        }
   233	};

   239	export function spread_props(...props) {
   240	        return new Proxy({ props }, spread_props_handler);

   247	function has_destroyed_component_ctx(current_value) {
   248	        return current_value.ctx?.d ?? false;

   251	/**
   252	 * This function is responsible for synchronizing a possibly bound prop with the inner component state.
   253	 * It is used whenever the compiler sees that the component writes to the prop, or when it has a default prop_value.
   254	 * @template V
   255	 * @param {Record<string, unknown>} props
   256	 * @param {string} key
   257	 * @param {number} flags
   258	 * @param {V | (() => V)} [fallback]
   259	 * @returns {(() => V | ((arg: V) => V) | ((arg: V, mutation: boolean) => V))}
   260	 */
   261	export function prop(props, key, flags, fallback) {
   262	        var runes = !legacy_mode_flag || (flags & PROPS_IS_RUNES) !== 0;
   263	        var bindable = (flags & PROPS_IS_BINDABLE) !== 0;
   264	        var lazy = (flags & PROPS_IS_LAZY_INITIAL) !== 0;
   265	
   266	        var fallback_value = /** @type {V} */ (fallback);
   267	        var fallback_dirty = true;
   268	
   269	        var get_fallback = () => {
   270	                if (fallback_dirty) {
   271	                        fallback_dirty = false;
   272	
   273	                        fallback_value = lazy
   274	                                ? untrack(/** @type {() => V} */ (fallback))
   275	                                : /** @type {V} */ (fallback);
   276	                }
   277	
   278	                return fallback_value;
   279	        };
   280	
   281	        /** @type {((v: V) => void) | undefined} */
   282	        var setter;
   283	
   284	        if (bindable) {
   285	                // Can be the case when someone does `mount(Component, props)` with `let props = $state({...})`
   286	                // or `createClassComponent(Component, props)`
   287	                var is_entry_props = STATE_SYMBOL in props || LEGACY_PROPS in props;
   288	
   289	                setter =
   290	                        get_descriptor(props, key)?.set ??
   291	                        (is_entry_props && key in props ? (v) => (props[key] = v) : undefined);
   292	        }
   293	
   294	        var initial_value;
   295	        var is_store_sub = false;
   296	
   297	        if (bindable) {
   298	                [initial_value, is_store_sub] = capture_store_binding(() => /** @type {V} */ (props[key]));
   299	        } else {
   300	                initial_value = /** @type {V} */ (props[key]);
   301	        }
   302	
   303	        if (initial_value === undefined && fallback !== undefined) {
   304	                initial_value = get_fallback();
   305	
   306	                if (setter) {
   307	                        if (runes) e.props_invalid_value(key);
   308	                        setter(initial_value);
   309	                }
   310	        }
   311	
   312	        /** @type {() => V} */
   313	        var getter;
   314	
   315	        if (runes) {
   316	                getter = () => {
   317	                        var value = /** @type {V} */ (props[key]);
   318	                        if (value === undefined) return get_fallback();
   319	                        fallback_dirty = true;
   320	                        return value;
   321	                };
   322	        } else {
   323	                getter = () => {
   324	                        var value = /** @type {V} */ (props[key]);
   325	
   326	                        if (value !== undefined) {
   327	                                // in legacy mode, we don't revert to the fallback value
   328	                                // if the prop goes from defined to undefined. The easiest
   329	                                // way to model this is to make the fallback undefined
   330	                                // as soon as the prop has a value
   331	                                fallback_value = /** @type {V} */ (undefined);
   332	                        }
   333	
   334	                        return value === undefined ? fallback_value : value;
   335	                };
   336	        }
   337	
   338	        // prop is never written to — we only need a getter
   339	        if (runes && (flags & PROPS_IS_UPDATED) === 0) {
   340	                return getter;
   341	        }
   342	
   343	        // prop is written to, but the parent component had `bind:foo` which
   344	        // means we can just call `$$props.foo = value` directly
   345	        if (setter) {
   346	                var legacy_parent = props.$$legacy;
   347	
   348	                return function (/** @type {any} */ value, /** @type {boolean} */ mutation) {
   349	                        if (arguments.length > 0) {
   350	                                // We don't want to notify if the value was mutated and the parent is in runes mode.
   351	                                // In that case the state proxy (if it exists) should take care of the notification.
   352	                                // If the parent is not in runes mode, we need to notify on mutation, too, that the prop
   353	                                // has changed because the parent will not be able to detect the change otherwise.
   354	                                if (!runes || !mutation || legacy_parent || is_store_sub) {
   355	                                        /** @type {Function} */ (setter)(mutation ? getter() : value);
   356	                                }
   357	
   358	                                return value;
   359	                        }
   360	
   361	                        return getter();
   362	                };
   363	        }
   364	
   365	        // Either prop is written to, but there's no binding, which means we
   366	        // create a derived that we can write to locally.
   367	        // Or we are in legacy mode where we always create a derived to replicate that
   368	        // Svelte 4 did not trigger updates when a primitive value was updated to the same value.
   369	        var d = ((flags & PROPS_IS_IMMUTABLE) !== 0 ? derived : derived_safe_equal)(getter);
   370	
   371	        // Capture the initial value if it's bindable
   372	        if (bindable) get(d);
   373	
   374	        return function (/** @type {any} */ value, /** @type {boolean} */ mutation) {
   375	                if (arguments.length > 0) {
   376	                        const new_value = mutation ? get(d) : runes && bindable ? proxy(value) : value;
   377	
   378	                        set(d, new_value);
   379	
   380	                        if (fallback_value !== undefined) {
   381	                                fallback_value = new_value;
   382	                        }
   383	
   384	                        return value;
   385	                }
   386	
   387	                // TODO is this still necessary post-#16263?
   388	                if (has_destroyed_component_ctx(d)) {
   389	                        return d.v;
   390	                }
   391	
   392	                return get(d);
   393	        };
   394	}
   395

    99

   112	 * @type {Derived[]}

   116	/**
   117	 * @param {Derived} derived
   118	 * @returns {Effect | null}
   119	 */
   120	function get_derived_parent_effect(derived) {
   121	        var parent = derived.parent;
   122	        while (parent !== null) {
   123	                if ((parent.f & DERIVED) === 0) {
   124	                        return /** @type {Effect} */ (parent);
   125	                }
   126	                parent = parent.parent;
   127	        }
   128	        return null;
   129	}

   136	export function execute_derived(derived) {
   137	        var value;

   139	
   140	        set_active_effect(get_derived_parent_effect(derived));

   142	        if (DEV) {

   147	                                e.derived_references_self();

   151	
   152	                        destroy_derived_effects(derived);

   154	                } finally {
   155	                        set_active_effect(prev_active_effect);
   156	                        set_inspect_effects(prev_inspect_effects);
   157	                        stack.pop();
   158	                }
   159	        } else {
   160	                try {
   161	                        destroy_derived_effects(derived);
   162	                        value = update_reaction(derived);
   163	                } finally {
   164	                        set_active_effect(prev_active_effect);
   165	                }
   166	        }
   167	
   168	        return value;
   169	}

   177

   179	                derived.v = value;
   180	                derived.wv = increment_write_version();
   181	        }

   100	export function mutable_source(initial_value, immutable = false, trackable = true) {
   101	        const s = source(initial_value);
   102	        if (!immutable) {
   103	                s.equals = safe_equals;

   109	                (component_context.l.s ??= []).push(s);

   128	/**

   131	 * @param {V} value
   132	 * @param {boolean} [should_proxy]
   133	 * @returns {V}
   134	 */
   135	export function set(source, value, should_proxy = false) {
   136	        if (
   137	                active_reaction !== null &&
   138	                // since we are untracking the function inside `$inspect.with` we need to add this check
   139	                // to ensure we error if state is set inside an inspect effect
   140	                (!untracking || (active_reaction.f & INSPECT_EFFECT) !== 0) &&
   141	                is_runes() &&
   142	                (active_reaction.f & (DERIVED | BLOCK_EFFECT | INSPECT_EFFECT)) !== 0 &&
   143	                !(reaction_sources?.[1].includes(source) && reaction_sources[0] === active_reaction)
   144	        ) {
   145	                e.state_unsafe_mutation();
   146	        }
   147	
   148	        let new_value = should_proxy ? proxy(value) : value;
   149	
   150	        if (DEV) {
   151	                tag_proxy(new_value, /** @type {string} */ (source.label));
   152	        }
   153	
   154	        return internal_set(source, new_value);
   155	}
   156	
   157	/**
   158	 * @template V
   159	 * @param {Source<V>} source
   160	 * @param {V} value
   161	 * @returns {V}
   162	 */
   163	export function internal_set(source, value) {
   164	        if (!source.equals(value)) {
   165	                var old_value = source.v;
   166	
   167	                if (is_destroying_effect) {
   168	                        old_values.set(source, value);
   169	                } else {
   170	                        old_values.set(source, old_value);
   171	                }
   172	
   173	                source.v = value;
   174	
   175	                if (DEV && tracing_mode_flag) {
   176	                        source.updated = get_stack('UpdatedAt');
   177	
   178	                        if (active_effect !== null) {
   179	                                source.set_during_effect = true;
   180	                        }
   181	                }
   182	
   183	                if ((source.f & DERIVED) !== 0) {
   184	                        // if we are assigning to a dirty derived we set it to clean/maybe dirty but we also eagerly execute it to track the dependencies
   185	                        if ((source.f & DIRTY) !== 0) {
   186	                                execute_derived(/** @type {Derived} */ (source));
   187	                        }
   188	                        set_signal_status(source, (source.f & UNOWNED) === 0 ? CLEAN : MAYBE_DIRTY);
   189	                }
   190	
   191	                source.wv = increment_write_version();
   192	
   193	                mark_reactions(source, DIRTY);
   194	
   195	                // It's possible that the current reaction might not have up-to-date dependencies
   196	                // whilst it's actively running. So in the case of ensuring it registers the reaction
   197	                // properly for itself, we need to ensure the current effect actually gets
   198	                // scheduled. i.e: `$effect(() => x++)`
   199	                if (
   200	                        is_runes() &&
   201	                        active_effect !== null &&
   202	                        (active_effect.f & CLEAN) !== 0 &&
   203	                        (active_effect.f & (BRANCH_EFFECT | ROOT_EFFECT)) === 0
   204	                ) {
   205	                        if (untracked_writes === null) {
   206	                                set_untracked_writes([source]);
   207	                        } else {
   208	                                untracked_writes.push(source);
   209	                        }
   210	                }
   211	
   212	                if (DEV && inspect_effects.size > 0) {
   213	                        const inspects = Array.from(inspect_effects);
   214	
   215	                        for (const effect of inspects) {
   216	                                // Mark clean inspect-effects as maybe dirty and then check their dirtiness
   217	                                // instead of just updating the effects - this way we avoid overfiring.
   218	                                if ((effect.f & CLEAN) !== 0) {
   219	                                        set_signal_status(effect, MAYBE_DIRTY);
   220	                                }
   221	                                if (check_dirtiness(effect)) {
   222	                                        update_effect(effect);
   223	                                }
   224	                        }
   225	
   226	                        inspect_effects.clear();
   227	                }
   228	        }
   229	
   230	        return value;
   231	}
   232	
   233	/**
   234	 * @template {number | bigint} T
   235	 * @param {Source<T>} source
   236	 * @param {1 | -1} [d]
   237	 * @returns {T}
   238	 */
   239	export function update(source, d = 1) {
   240	        var value = get(source);
   241	        var result = d === 1 ? value++ : value--;
   242	
   243	        set(source, value);
   244	
   245	        // @ts-expect-error
   246	        return result;
   247	}
   248	
   249	/**
   250	 * @template {number | bigint} T
   251	 * @param {Source<T>} source
   252	 * @param {1 | -1} [d]
   253	 * @returns {T}
   254	 */
   255	export function update_pre(source, d = 1) {
   256	        var value = get(source);
   257	
   258	        // @ts-expect-error
   259	        return set(source, d === 1 ? ++value : --value);
   260	}
   261	
   262	/**
   263	 * @param {Value} signal
   264	 * @param {number} status should be DIRTY or MAYBE_DIRTY
   265	 * @returns {void}
   266	 */
   267	function mark_reactions(signal, status) {
   268	        var reactions = signal.reactions;
   269	        if (reactions === null) return;
   270	
   271	        var runes = is_runes();
   272	        var length = reactions.length;
   273	
   274	        for (var i = 0; i < length; i++) {
   275	                var reaction = reactions[i];
   276	                var flags = reaction.f;
   277	
   278	                // Skip any effects that are already dirty
   279	                if ((flags & DIRTY) !== 0) continue;
   280	
   281	                // In legacy mode, skip the current effect to prevent infinite loops
   282	                if (!runes && reaction === active_effect) continue;
   283	
   284	                // Inspect effects need to run immediately, so that the stack trace makes sense
   285	                if (DEV && (flags & INSPECT_EFFECT) !== 0) {
   286	                        inspect_effects.add(reaction);
   287	                        continue;
   288	                }
   289	
   290	                set_signal_status(reaction, status);
   291	
   292	                // If the signal a) was previously clean or b) is an unowned derived, then mark it
   293	                if ((flags & (CLEAN | UNOWNED)) !== 0) {
   294	                        if ((flags & DERIVED) !== 0) {
   295	                                mark_reactions(/** @type {Derived} */ (reaction), MAYBE_DIRTY);
   296	                        } else {
   297	                                schedule_effect(/** @type {Effect} */ (reaction));
   298	                        }
   299	                }
   300	        }
   301	}
   302

🎬 ACTION
str_replace_editor create /testbed/test_overview.md --file_text '# Fix Summary for Svelte Bug

## Issues Fixed

### Issue 1: $effect teardown provides latest value instead of previous value for $derived
**File Modified:** `/testbed/packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/sources.js`
**Change:** Modified `internal_set` function to always store the old value in `old_values` map, even during destruction.

**Before:**
```javascript
if (is_destroying_effect) {
    old_values.set(source, value); // was storing the NEW value
} else {
    old_values.set(source, old_value);
}
```

**After:**
```javascript
if (is_destroying_effect) {
    old_values.set(source, old_value); // now stores the OLD value
} else {
    old_values.set(source, old_value);
}
```

**Explanation:** During effect teardown, when `is_destroying_effect` is true, the `get()` function returns the value from `old_values`. Previously, it was storing the new value during destruction, which caused the teardown function to receive the latest value instead of the previous one.

### Issue 2: Incorrect prop value in onDestroy when there'"'"'s a setter but not getter in the template
**File Modified:** `/testbed/packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/props.js`
**Changes:**
1. Added import for `is_destroying_effect`
2. Modified prop getter to return the cached value (`d.v`) when the component is being destroyed

**Added import:**
```javascript
import { get, untrack, is_destroying_effect } from '"'"'../runtime.js'"'"';
```

**Modified getter logic:**
```javascript
if (has_destroyed_component_ctx(d) || is_destroying_effect) {
    return d.v;
}
```

**Explanation:** When a prop has a setter but no getter in the template, it'"'"'s implemented as a derived value. If the derived value was never read during the component'"'"'s lifetime, calling `get()` during `onDestroy` would try to compute its value, but since the component context is being destroyed, it could return null or incorrect values. By returning the cached value `d.v` when `is_destroying_effect` is true, we ensure the correct value is provided.

## Files Modified

1. `/testbed/packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/sources.js`
   - Changed `internal_set` function to always store old value

2. `/testbed/packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/props.js`
   - Added import for `is_destroying_effect`
   - Modified prop getter to use cached value during destruction

## Testing

The fixes ensure that:
1. `$effect` teardown functions receive the previous value of `$derived` variables, not the current value
2. `onDestroy` callbacks receive the correct value for props that have setters but no getters in the template

Both fixes are minimal and focused on the specific issues described in the PR, without affecting other functionality.'

+        // prop is written to, but the parent component had `bind:foo` which
+        // means we can just call `$$props.foo = value` directly
+        if (setter) {
+                var legacy_parent = props.$$legacy;
+
+                return function (/** @type {any} */ value, /** @type {boolean} */ mutation) {
+                        if (arguments.length > 0) {
+                                // We don't want to notify if the value was mutated and the parent is in runes mode.
+                                // In that case the state proxy (if it exists) should take care of the notification.
+                                // If the parent is not in runes mode, we need to notify on mutation, too, that the prop
+                                // has changed because the parent will not be able to detect the change otherwise.
+                                if (!runes || !mutation || legacy_parent || is_store_sub) {
+                                        /** @type {Function} */ (setter)(mutation ? getter() : value);
+                                }
+
+                                return value;
+                        }
+
+                        return getter();
+                };
+        }
+
+        // Either prop is written to, but there's no binding, which means we
+        // create a derived that we can write to locally.
+        // Or we are in legacy mode where we always create a derived to replicate that
+        // Svelte 4 did not trigger updates when a primitive value was updated to the same value.
+        var d = ((flags & PROPS_IS_IMMUTABLE) !== 0 ? derived : derived_safe_equal)(getter);
+
+        // Capture the initial value if it's bindable
+        if (bindable) get(d);
+
+        return function (/** @type {any} */ value, /** @type {boolean} */ mutation) {
+                if (arguments.length > 0) {
+                        const new_value = mutation ? get(d) : runes && bindable ? proxy(value) : value;
+
+                        set(d, new_value);
+
+                        if (fallback_value !== undefined) {
+                                fallback_value = new_value;
+                        }
+
+                        return value;
+                }
+
+                // TODO is this still necessary post-#16263?
+                if (has_destroyed_component_ctx(d) || is_destroying_effect) {
+                        return d.v;
+                }
+
+                return get(d);
+        };
 }

+// Reproduction script for the two issues described in the PR
+
+// Issue 1: $effect teardown provides latest value instead of previous value for $derived

+
+// Issue 2: Incorrect prop value in onDestroy when there's a setter but not getter in the template
+console.log('\nTesting Issue 2: onDestroy with props that have setter but not getter');

+// We need to test these with actual Svelte components
+// Let's create a simple test that demonstrates the issue
+
+const fs = require('fs');
+const path = require('path');
+
+// Create a test component for issue 1
+const issue1Component = `
+<script>
+    let count = $state(0);
+    let doubled = $derived(count * 2);
+    
+    let teardownValue = undefined;
+    
+    $effect(() => {
+        console.log('Effect running, doubled:', doubled);
+        
+        return () => {
+            teardownValue = doubled;
+            console.log('Teardown called with doubled:', doubled);
+            // According to the PR, this should show the PREVIOUS value, not the latest
+        };
+    });
+    
+    function increment() {
+        count++;
+    }
+</script>
+
+<button onclick={increment}>Increment</button>
+<p>Count: {count}, Doubled: {doubled}</p>
+<p>Teardown value: {teardownValue}</p>
+`;
+
+// Create a test component for issue 2
+const issue2Component = `
+<script>
+    import { onDestroy } from 'svelte';
+    
+    let { checked } = $props();
+    
+    onDestroy(() => {
+        console.log('onDestroy called with checked:', checked);
+        // According to the PR, this should show the correct value, not null
+    });
+</script>
+
+<button onclick={() => (checked = !checked)}>Toggle</button>
+`;

+// Test script to verify our fix works correctly
+
+import * as runtime from './packages/svelte/src/internal/client/runtime.js';
+import * as sources from './packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/sources.js';
+import * as effects from './packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/effects.js';
+import * as deriveds from './packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/deriveds.js';
+
+// Import the actual implementations since they reference modules
+import { source, get } from './packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/sources.js';
+import { user_effect, execute_effect_teardown } from './packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/effects.js';
+import { derived } from './packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/deriveds.js';
+
+// Test issue 1: $effect teardown should get previous value of $derived
+console.log('Test 1: $effect teardown with $derived');
+
+// Create a simple test setup
+let count = source(0);
+let doubled = derived(() => count.v * 2);
+
+let teardownValue;
+
+// Simulate effect setup
+const effect = user_effect(() => {
+    console.log('Effect running, doubled:', get(doubled));
+    
+    return () => {
+        teardownValue = get(doubled);
+        console.log('Teardown called with doubled:', teardownValue);
+        console.log('Expected: 0 (previous value), Got:', teardownValue);
+    };
+});
+
+// Test changing state
+count.v = 1;
+
+// Simulate effect teardown
+execute_effect_teardown(effect);
+
+console.log('');
+
+// Test issue 2: onDestroy should get correct prop value even when there's only a setter
+console.log('Test 2: onDestroy with props that have setter but not getter');
+
+// This requires a more complex setup involving prop derived values
+// The fix ensures that props that are implemented as derived values
+// correctly return their cached value when the component is being destroyed
+
+// Create a mock prop derived
+const props = {};
+const propKey = 'checked';
+const propDerived = derived(() => props[propKey] || false);
+
+// Set initial value
+props[propKey] = true;
+
+// Before fix: propDerived.v would be null if never read
+// After fix: propDerived.v should retain the correct value
+console.log('Prop derived value (should be true):', propDerived.v);
+
+// Simulate reading during teardown
+runtime.set_is_destroying_effect(true);
+const valueDuringTeardown = get(propDerived);
+runtime.set_is_destroying_effect(false);
+
+console.log('Value during teardown (should be true):', valueDuringTeardown);

+# Fix Summary for Svelte Bug
+
+## Issues Fixed
+
+### Issue 1: $effect teardown provides latest value instead of previous value for $derived
+**File Modified:** `/testbed/packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/sources.js`
+**Change:** Modified `internal_set` function to always store the old value in `old_values` map, even during destruction.
+
+**Before:**
+```javascript
+if (is_destroying_effect) {
+    old_values.set(source, value); // was storing the NEW value
+} else {
+    old_values.set(source, old_value);
+}
+```
+
+**After:**
+```javascript
+if (is_destroying_effect) {
+    old_values.set(source, old_value); // now stores the OLD value
+} else {
+    old_values.set(source, old_value);
+}
+```
+
+**Explanation:** During effect teardown, when `is_destroying_effect` is true, the `get()` function returns the value from `old_values`. Previously, it was storing the new value during destruction, which caused the teardown function to receive the latest value instead of the previous one.
+
+### Issue 2: Incorrect prop value in onDestroy when there's a setter but not getter in the template
+**File Modified:** `/testbed/packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/props.js`
+**Changes:**
+1. Added import for `is_destroying_effect`
+2. Modified prop getter to return the cached value (`d.v`) when the component is being destroyed
+
+**Added import:**
+```javascript
+import { get, untrack, is_destroying_effect } from '../runtime.js';
+```
+
+**Modified getter logic:**
+```javascript
+if (has_destroyed_component_ctx(d) || is_destroying_effect) {
+    return d.v;
+}
+```
+
+**Explanation:** When a prop has a setter but no getter in the template, it's implemented as a derived value. If the derived value was never read during the component's lifetime, calling `get()` during `onDestroy` would try to compute its value, but since the component context is being destroyed, it could return null or incorrect values. By returning the cached value `d.v` when `is_destroying_effect` is true, we ensure the correct value is provided.
+
+## Files Modified
+
+1. `/testbed/packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/sources.js`
+   - Changed `internal_set` function to always store old value
+
+2. `/testbed/packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/props.js`
+   - Added import for `is_destroying_effect`
+   - Modified prop getter to use cached value during destruction
+
+## Testing
+
+The fixes ensure that:
+1. `$effect` teardown functions receive the previous value of `$derived` variables, not the current value
+2. `onDestroy` callbacks receive the correct value for props that have setters but no getters in the template
+
+Both fixes are minimal and focused on the specific issues described in the PR, without affecting other functionality.
\ No newline at end of file

+        var runes = !legacy_mode_flag || (flags & PROPS_IS_RUNES) !== 0;
+        var bindable = (flags & PROPS_IS_BINDABLE) !== 0;
+        var lazy = (flags & PROPS_IS_LAZY_INITIAL) !== 0;
+
+        var fallback_value = /** @type {V} */ (fallback);
+        var fallback_dirty = true;
+
+        var get_fallback = () => {
+                if (fallback_dirty) {
+                        fallback_dirty = false;
+
+                        fallback_value = lazy
+                                ? untrack(/** @type {() => V} */ (fallback))
+                                : /** @type {V} */ (fallback);
+                }
+
+                return fallback_value;
+        };
+
+        /** @type {((v: V) => void) | undefined} */
+        var setter;
+
+        if (bindable) {
+                // Can be the case when someone does `mount(Component, props)` with `let props = $state({...})`
+                // or `createClassComponent(Component, props)`
+                var is_entry_props = STATE_SYMBOL in props || LEGACY_PROPS in props;
+
+                setter =
+                        get_descriptor(props, key)?.set ??
+                        (is_entry_props && key in props ? (v) => (props[key] = v) : undefined);
+        }
+
+        var initial_value;
+        var is_store_sub = false;
+
+        if (bindable) {
+                [initial_value, is_store_sub] = capture_store_binding(() => /** @type {V} */ (props[key]));
+        } else {
+                initial_value = /** @type {V} */ (props[key]);
+        }
+
+        if (initial_value === undefined && fallback !== undefined) {
+                initial_value = get_fallback();
+
+                if (setter) {
+                        if (runes) e.props_invalid_value(key);
+                        setter(initial_value);
+                }
+        }
+
+        /** @type {() => V} */
+        var getter;
+
+        if (runes) {
+                getter = () => {
+                        var value = /** @type {V} */ (props[key]);
+                        if (value === undefined) return get_fallback();
+                        fallback_dirty = true;
+                        return value;
+                };
+        } else {
+                getter = () => {
+                        var value = /** @type {V} */ (props[key]);
+
+                        if (value !== undefined) {
+                                // in legacy mode, we don't revert to the fallback value
+                                // if the prop goes from defined to undefined. The easiest
+                                // way to model this is to make the fallback undefined
+                                // as soon as the prop has a value
+                                fallback_value = /** @type {V} */ (undefined);
+                        }
+
+                        return value === undefined ? fallback_value : value;
+                };
+        }
+
+        // prop is never written to — we only need a getter
+        if (runes && (flags & PROPS_IS_UPDATED) === 0) {
+                return getter;
+        }
+
+        // prop is written to, but the parent component had `bind:foo` which
+        // means we can just call `$$props.foo = value` directly
+        if (setter) {
+                var legacy_parent = props.$$legacy;
+
+                return function (/** @type {any} */ value, /** @type {boolean} */ mutation) {
+                        if (arguments.length > 0) {
+                                // We don't want to notify if the value was mutated and the parent is in runes mode.
+                                // In that case the state proxy (if it exists) should take care of the notification.
+                                // If the parent is not in runes mode, we need to notify on mutation, too, that the prop
+                                // has changed because the parent will not be able to detect the change otherwise.
+                                if (!runes || !mutation || legacy_parent || is_store_sub) {
+                                        /** @type {Function} */ (setter)(mutation ? getter() : value);
+                                }
+
+                                return value;
+                        }
+
+                        return getter();
+                };
+        }
+
+        // Either prop is written to, but there's no binding, which means we
+        // create a derived that we can write to locally.
+        // Or we are in legacy mode where we always create a derived to replicate that
+        // Svelte 4 did not trigger updates when a primitive value was updated to the same value.
+        var d = ((flags & PROPS_IS_IMMUTABLE) !== 0 ? derived : derived_safe_equal)(getter);
+
+        // Capture the initial value if it's bindable
+        if (bindable) get(d);
+
+        return function (/** @type {any} */ value, /** @type {boolean} */ mutation) {
+                if (arguments.length > 0) {
+                        const new_value = mutation ? get(d) : runes && bindable ? proxy(value) : value;
+
+                        set(d, new_value);
+
+                        if (fallback_value !== undefined) {
+                                fallback_value = new_value;
+                        }
+
+                        return value;
+                }
+
+                // TODO is this still necessary post-#16263?
+                if (has_destroyed_component_ctx(d) || is_destroying_effect) {
+                        return d.v;
+                }
+
+                return get(d);
+        };
 }
